ba
=
$('.video-ba-content');








var
h
=
$(window).height();








var
s
=
$(window).scrollTop();








var
min;








var
holder;








$('.video-ba-placeholder:visible').each(function
(){










var
curTop
=
$(this).offset().top;










var
d
=
Math.abs(h
-
2*(curTop+200-s));










if
(
!holder
||
d
<
min)
{












holder
=
$(this);












min
=
d;










}








});









if
(holder
&&
holder.attr('id')!=ba.parent().attr('id')){










ba.fadeOut(1000,
function(){

holder.append(ba.fadeIn(1500));










})








}






}
catch
(all){






}




},
5000);
